                                                    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text">
                                                        <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto">
                                                            <h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">程序员做饭指南</h1>
                                                            <a id="user-content-程序员做饭指南" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 程序员做饭指南" href="#程序员做饭指南">
                                                                <svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">
                                                                    <path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path>
                                                                </svg>
                                                            </a>
                                                        </div>
                                                        <p dir="auto">
                                                            <a href="https://github.com/Anduin2017/HowToCook/actions/workflows/build.yml">
                                                                <img src="https://github.com/Anduin2017/HowToCook/actions/workflows/build.yml/badge.svg" alt="build" style="max-width: 100%;">
                                                            </a>
                                                            <a href="/Anduin2017/HowToCook/blob/master/LICENSE">
                                                                <img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c69f2eef6f1182df8d054868ecfca7ea8ea2109fe9fb8e9aec6afa7e376e5530/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6769746875622f6c6963656e73652f416e6475696e323031372f486f77546f436f6f6b" alt="License" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/github/license/Anduin2017/HowToCook" style="max-width: 100%;">
                                                            </a>
                                                            <a href="https://github.com/Anduin2017/HowToCook/graphs/contributors">
                                                                <img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/6a07b230b2e67d9b8700d8dfbed9a1e60090cf365f049c21e33a0eb7806c987f/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6769746875622f636f6e7472696275746f72732f416e6475696e323031372f486f77546f436f6f6b" alt="GitHub contributors" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/github/contributors/Anduin2017/HowToCook" style="max-width: 100%;">
                                                            </a>
                                                            <a href="https://www.npmjs.com/package/how-to-cook" rel="nofollow">
                                                                <img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/2b1c990479bb94baf0b69192f22d7d3fb821cd0fcb9a3a833395604d128c35e8/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f6e706d2f762f686f772d746f2d636f6f6b" alt="npm" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/npm/v/how-to-cook" style="max-width: 100%;">
                                                            </a>
                                                            <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" href="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/423c9ef046e80fbb5d632f19f490baea7c5acd81eee636002fbf5c721a8a6137/68747470733a2f2f6d616e686f7572732e61697572736f66742e636f6d2f722f6769746875622e636f6d2f616e6475696e323031372f686f77746f636f6f6b2e737667">
                                                                <img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/423c9ef046e80fbb5d632f19f490baea7c5acd81eee636002fbf5c721a8a6137/68747470733a2f2f6d616e686f7572732e61697572736f66742e636f6d2f722f6769746875622e636f6d2f616e6475696e323031372f686f77746f636f6f6b2e737667" alt="Man hours" data-canonical-src="https://manhours.aiursoft.com/r/github.com/anduin2017/howtocook.svg" style="max-width: 100%;">
                                                            </a>
                                                            <a href="https://github.com/Anduin2017/HowToCook/pkgs/container/how-to-cook">
                                                                <img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/4cf7ba716f6203978f87eb6f8e1c089ce535ef717e6daa3680c5e248c506152f/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f646f636b65722d6c61746573742d626c75653f6c6f676f3d646f636b6572" alt="Docker" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/docker-latest-blue?logo=docker" style="max-width: 100%;">
                                                            </a>
                                                            <a href="https://rvlt.gg/ndApqZEs" rel="nofollow">
                                                                <img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/a8b2e4a4c260dd5bffbce6343703f0b061afc094e8643fb23ee0152108217ff1/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f5265766f6c742d4a6f696e2d6664363637313f7374796c653d666c61742d737175617265" alt="Join the AnduinOS Community on Revolt" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/Revolt-Join-fd6671?style=flat-square" style="max-width: 100%;">
                                                            </a>
                                                        </p>
                                                        <p dir="auto">最近宅在家做饭，作为程序员，我偶尔在网上找找菜谱和做法。但是这些菜谱往往写法千奇百怪，经常中间莫名出来一些材料。对于习惯了形式语言的程序员来说极其不友好。</p>
                                                        <p dir="auto">所以，我计划自己搜寻菜谱并结合实际做菜的经验，准备用更清晰精准的描述来整理常见菜的做法，以方便程序员在家做饭。</p>
                                                        <p dir="auto">同样，我希望它是一个由社区驱动和维护的开源项目，使更多人能够一起做一个有趣的仓库。所以非常欢迎大家贡献它~</p>
                                                        <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto">
                                                            <h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">本地部署</h2>
                                                            <a id="user-content-本地部署" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 本地部署" href="#本地部署">
                                                                <svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">
                                                                    <path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path>
                                                                </svg>
                                                            </a>
                                                        </div>
                                                        <p dir="auto">如果需要在本地部署菜谱 Web 服务，可以在安装 Docker 后运行下面命令：</p>
                                                        <div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="docker pull ghcr.io/anduin2017/how-to-cook:latest
docker run -d -p 5000:80 ghcr.io/anduin2017/how-to-cook:latest">
                                                            <pre>docker pull ghcr.io/anduin2017/how-to-cook:latest
docker run -d -p 5000:80 ghcr.io/anduin2017/how-to-cook:latest</pre>
                                                        </div>
                                                        <p dir="auto">
                                                            如需下载 PDF 版本，可以在浏览器中访问 <a href="https://cook.aiursoft.com/document.pdf" rel="nofollow">/document.pdf</a>
                                                        </p>
                                                        <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto">
                                                            <h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">如何贡献</h2>
                                                            <a id="user-content-如何贡献" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 如何贡献" href="#如何贡献">
                                                                <svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">
                                                                    <path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path>
                                                                </svg>
                                                            </a>
                                                        </div>
                                                        <p dir="auto">针对发现的问题，直接修改并提交 Pull request 即可。</p>
                                                        <p dir="auto">
                                                            在写新菜谱时，请复制并修改已有的菜谱模板: <a href="https://github.com/Anduin2017/HowToCook/blob/master/dishes/template/%E7%A4%BA%E4%BE%8B%E8%8F%9C/%E7%A4%BA%E4%BE%8B%E8%8F%9C.md?plain=1">示例菜</a>
                                                            。
                                                        </p>
                                                        <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto">
                                                            <h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">搭建环境</h2>
